< Review>
I rarely write positive reviews because quite frankly it‚Äôs seldom that I‚Äôm wowed by a customer service experience.  I needed the front break on my bike fixed and both of my tires were worn so I actually considered buying a new bike.  Instead I took my bike to Rooster Wheels in Marina with the goal of just getting the break fixed. The proprietor (William) was super friendly and indicated he could fix the break on the spot. He commented on the tires and I elected to leave the bike there for him to install new ones (tubes and tires). Less than 2 hours later he calls and tells me my bike is ready.  A break fixed, two new tires, prompt and friendly service -- $25. Wow, what a bargain!< /Review>

< Review>
I'm actually really sad to hear that they will be renovating this place and making it exclusive. I'm really fortunate to have visited this hotel in its current incarnation. I would have liked to visit again on my next trip to LA. The room itself was literally bigger than my apartment! We really loved the layout. The decor was really nice and the ambience was really cool. The service was really good. One staff member even let us see the library (which was closed at the time) before we left since we missed getting in the night before. I would have loved to explore the hotel a little more. The only reason I am giving 5 stars is their website states they have a car service within 3 miles of the hotel, which was a really strong amenity to get me to book the place, but when we got there, the car service was not available so we wound up getting Lyft rides mostly. All in all it seems like a really cool place and I'll be sad to have to find a new hotel next time I am in town.</Review>

<rate>4< /rate>< Text>
Unique, trendy hotel. Staff seemed inexperienced as far as hospitality industry goes. Stayed on a Thursday night, which is essentially the new Friday night for many people these days. The bar and restaurant were closed by 11pm. The front desk said that the hotel offered 24 hour room service, either from their own facilities or from local delivery service like door dash or eat24. However, when we called at 12:30, no one answered. Anywhere. Not even the front desk. I loved the room- the layout, decor, location. We would have planned for other dining options had we known there were none available.<//Text>

The building was originally built to be condos so the hotel rooms are very spacious with an open floor plan that includes a full kitchen. If you stay here, don't get an interior room overlooking the library patio. The view is nice but the soundproof windows/balcony door does not work. The live band and DJ kept me up past midnight and I had to be up at 5:00 the next morning. I stay here with friends whenever I'm in town and I have friends playing the venue next door. <Name>Nicole Torres<//Name><review>‚ÄúGreat hotel & location!‚Äù
I found this place back in June when I was starting to plan my trip out to the West Coast and after booking the hotel and a few emails back and forth with Bryan (who is excellent!), I felt completely confident with my choice. I had seen that there could be issues with noise from TA and so had paid in advance to upgrade to a room on the other side of the building. Once we got there, we got offered to either take that room or a different upgrade - to a Hollywood Premier Suite which was also incredibly quiet although lacking the view of the Hollywood sign/Capitol Records building. We went to see the room and were blown away by the size of it - 850 sq ft made you feel like you were in an apartment rather than a hotel room.

The main reasons this hotel gets a 5* rating from me are:
- Staff. They are absolutely wonderful and can't do enough for you. We're two late-20s girls and they told us where to head for nightlife/bars and were spot on for what we wanted.
- Location. Close enough to Hollywood but avoiding most of the tourist traffic which is a godsend. If you do the Hop On/Hop Off with Starline there's a bus stop around the block which saves you a 15 minute walk.
- Restaurant. Cleo was the best restaurant we ate at in Los Angeles and I'd go back in a heartbeat. It was buzzy, the food was brilliant & the bill was reasonable.
- Decoration. It's incredibly stylish and I loved the way the room was set out. My only gripe was the shower pressure wasn't brilliant although the rainfall shower was very cool.< /review><Date>1484726558673<//Date><Pics>None</Pics><userid>110763951031571640868< /userid><rate>5</rate>< Resp>

< text>
Unusual, eccentric, like an ageing hippy hotel. Spacious rooms, seductive (read dim) lighting with more switches than you can count on two hands, no bathtub in suite, vast flat wash basin designed by someone with more ambition than practical sense. Worst aspect is the noise. If overlooking courtyard, ghastly music blasts loudly on until 1.30am  Friday & Saturday. Other nights 11pm. Loudish music in all public areas including breakfast room at all times. nice staff, comfortable beds. You pays your money (quite a lot) and you takes your choice....< /text>

< review>
My husband booked The Redbury as a surprise part of our vacation based on the incredible TripAdvisor reviews. We arrived and were greeted by the very nice and helpful valet staff who, as you'll come to understand after reading further, were the best part of our entire stay at The Redbury.

We arrived late on a Saturday night in the midst of their busy night at their club/bar. Important to note that the bar/club extends from the first floor to the second, where the check-in desk is, so if you arrive on a Saturday night, you have to contend with the club crowd to check-in.

Upon checking in, we were greeted by a manager who gave us 2 room options, the room we had paid for; the room with the view of the Hollywood sign/Capitol Records building which he warned would be noisy, or a downgraded room in a quieter section of the building for no discount. We chose the quieter room which had some semblance of a view (as much as a 2nd floor could have), and began settling in.

Immediately we noticed cleanliness issues, not the least of which was an old blood stain on the pillowcase. We tried to overlook it, but upon turning the sheets down, found a bug. Not saying it was a bed beg, but it was an unidentified bug in the bed. We alerted the manager who assured us that they had no bed bug problem without viewing the bug in question, but he offered to move us to another room anyway. He moved us to a larger room on the same floor, but without any view which we had paid extra for. In addition, he assured us that we'd be taken care of with a bottle of champagne and breakfast which my husband graciously accepted. He also said he would check-in with us throughout our stay.

Sounds great, right? It did to us at the time. Our new room smelled clean (the first did not have this same smell), but then the problems continued. The toilet wasn't functioning properly, so at 1am (we had checked in at about 10pm, this ordeal lasted far too long), the manger brought a maintenance person to fix it. We were trying to settle in when we noticed hair stuck in the living room chairs, and were considering leaving. Having had to prepay for this entire stay, we had no choice but to give the manager a chance, and settled in (after checking the bed thoroughly :)) for the night.

The next morning I jumped into the large shower and while showering noticed there were about a half dozen or so stickers on the black tile wall. I figured out that they were from the shampoo bottles which have safety seals (the ones we were left were broken), so obviously other guests had peeled them off and stuck them to the wall and they weren't cleaned/removed.

Upon walking around the flat, it was clear that the rooms were badly in need of upkeep. The furniture had stains, the furniture was chipped/peeling, the drawers in the bathroom didn't function properly, counters were scratched, and the towels/linens were literally falling apart at the seams.

The next 4 nights were without major incident, however, we never received our champagne, our breakfast, and the manager who claimed to be so eager to make sure we had a great stay never checked in with us as he had promised he would.

A few days into our stay we noticed a $600 hold on the debit card we provided for "incidentals," a big deal when you're not alerted like every other hotel in the country does. As everyone knows, if you provide a card for incidentals, it's either charged about $100, or not at all. We prepaid, so there is no reason to put that kind of a hold on the card. I'd suspect that given the disrepair of the 2 rooms we saw, they are charging for damage quite often, and apparently not repairing it.

The highlight of The Redbury was, by far, the Valet staff who were extremely friendly and helpful. For the cost of this place, we could have stayed in a far nicer part of LA and had a much better experience. If you're looking to stay in this part of Hollywood, the W across the street looks like a far better option for a similar price (it's easily worth the few extra bucks).< /review>

<Rate>4< /Rate>< Review>
Great hotel and rooms, a film noir vibe and not your usual hotel. Room was spacious, with kitchen and bar area, lounge area with big TV, large comfortable bed and great walk in shower. Decor features alot of red, as in Redbury, everything was clean and well maintained. The location was good, if your after the area of Hollywood and Vine that is. The ground floor has the parking and a middle eastern restaurant, didn't try but looks nice and was busy. First floor has the reception/concierge (efficient and friendly) and a roof top bar and decked area (again didn't try but looked nice and was busy). The hotel is in a c shape so this covers the area in the middle. A short walk (10min) down Hollywood (follow the stars) gets you to highland with the dolby theater etc and views of the Hollywood sign. Across Vine Street is the Capitol Records building and quick access to the freeway 101. It's not a cheap stay but then what is these days and there are probably plenty of cheaper places around but all in all I didn't mind paying a bit more than I usually do, for the location and staying somewhere abit different.<//Review>

<Time>1349500417769<//Time><Rating>3< /Rating>< review>
Everyone else is right about the eclectic atmosphere, furnishings and ambiance.  This place is gorgeous and I really applaud SBE for their ability to combine authenticity with modern conveniences in a great location for any Hollywood visitor.

Unfortunately the service was very poor.  We booked in with our two kids and yet the room was only prepped for two (two towels, two bathrobes, etc.).  When we called to have the spare bed made up they sent a maid who spoke no English at all and made our kids' bed with just a sheet - she evidently thought they needed neither a quilt nor pillows!  When we called again half an hour later, they sent a guy with a really crappy attitude who just dumped the quilt and pillows on a chair, and turned on his heel and left the room without a word.  After calling a third time they sent that same guy back and he finally actually made the kids' bed.

We spent the next day out of the room for the whole day, leaving the "Please Make Up My Room" sign hanging on the door.  Evidently the maid with no English mistook that sign for the "Do Not Disturb" sign so when we returned to our room after a very busy and exhausting day, our room hadn't been made up.  Ack!

Add to this a few small things like that they make mention of wifi access in the _"Standard Amenities"_ section of their website, and yet that's the pathetic $10 per day gouge that any decent hotel includes for no extra these days, also the business center they talk about that was $5 for 15 minutes on a computer in an alcove in the lobby and printing was (I think) 50¬¢ per black & white page!  Both totally ridiculous fees considering what you pay.

I may as well round out my rant with some other sundries; it's just stupid to provide a spatula but no frypan, a cooking spoon but no saucepan, a chopping board but no carving knife, a mini bar with no pricelist, and a balcony with the airconditioning outlet (the hot air that goes outside) blowing at you!  Oh and "luxury bathrobe", you jest!<//review>

I heard about the cute Disney Park cups so I wanted to check it out.  They serve Starbucks drinks: Frappuccino, Smoothies, Espresso, Starbucks Refreshers, Teavana Iced Tea, Coffee, Tea, and pastries, etc. The lines are long but they go by fast. There are two sections inside, one for Starbucks items and the other side sells ice cream.

~Drinks~
I got my famous Green Tea Latte (Iced), they made it perfect.

~Customer Service~
To the point and quick.

~Highlight~
Cute cups!

~Rating~
If you're craving for Starbucks go here.  They made my Green Tea Latte (Iced), just right.  I would give it 4 Stars if the customer service was better.

~Notes~
~Seating is available inside and outside
~Located in California Adventure by the entrance</review>
